			| 0F9F0H: y := 0ECE1H
			| 0F9F1H: y := 0ECE4H
			| 0F9F2H..0F9F3H: y := x - 0D0BH
			| 0F9F4H..0F9F5H: y := x - 0CFDH
			| 0F9F6H: y := 0ECFAH
			| 0F9F7H..0F9F9H: y := x - 0C56H
			| 0F9FAH: y := 0EDEEH
			| 0F9FBH: y := 0EEDBH
			| 0F9FCH: y := 0F2BDH
			| 0F9FDH: y := 0F2FAH
			| 0F9FEH: y := 0F3B1H
			| 0F9FFH: y := 0F4A7H
			| 0FA00H: y := 0F4EEH
			| 0FA01H: y := 0F6F4H
			| 0FA02H: y := 0F6F6H
			| 0FA03H: y := 0F7B8H
			| 0FA04H: y := 0F7C8H
			| 0FA05H: y := 0F7D3H
			| 0FA06H: y := 0F8DBH
			| 0FA07H: y := 0F8F0H
			| 0FA08H..0FA09H: y := x + 99H
			| 0FA0AH: y := 0FAE6H
			| 0FA0BH: y := 0FCA9H
			| 0FF01H..0FF3BH: y := x - 5B60H
			| 0FF3CH: y := 0A1ACH
			| 0FF3DH..0FF5DH: y := x - 5B60H
			| 0FF5EH: y := 0A2A6H
			| 0FFE0H..0FFE1H: y := x - 5E15H
			| 0FFE2H: y := 0A1FEH
			| 0FFE3H: y := 0A3FEH
			| 0FFE5H: y := 0A1CDH
			| 0FFE6H: y := 0A3DCH
			ELSE
				RETURN
			END;
			IF y < 256 THEN
				t[tW] := SHORT(CHR(y)); INC(tW)
			ELSE
				t[tW] := SHORT(CHR(y DIV 100H)); t[tW+1] := SHORT(CHR(y MOD 100H)); INC(tW, 2)
			END;
			INC(fR); DEC(fLen)
		END
	END Encode;

	PROCEDURE NewEncoder* (): Codecs.Encoder;
		VAR e: Encoder;
	BEGIN
		NEW(e); RETURN e
	END NewEncoder;

	(* Decoder *)

	PROCEDURE (d: Decoder) Decode (IN f: ARRAY OF SHORTCHAR; VAR fR, fLen: INTEGER; VAR t: ARRAY OF CHAR; VAR tW: INTEGER; OUT state: BOOLEAN);
		VAR x, y: INTEGER;
	BEGIN
		WHILE fLen > 0 DO
			x := ORD(f[fR]);
			CASE d.st OF 0:
				CASE x OF
				| 00H..7FH: t[tW] := CHR(x); INC(tW)
				| 81H,82H,83H,84H,85H,86H,87H,88H,89H,8AH,8BH,8CH,8DH,8EH,8FH,90H,91H,92H,93H,94H,95H,96H,97H,98H,99H,9AH,9BH,9CH,9DH,9EH,9FH,0A0H,0A1H,0A2H,0A3H,0A4H,0A5H,0A6H,0A7H,0A8H,0A9H,0AAH,0ABH,0ACH,0ADH,0AEH,0AFH,0B0H,0B1H,0B2H,0B3H,0B4H,0B5H,0B6H,0B7H,0B8H,0B9H,0BAH,0BBH,0BCH,0BDH,0BEH,0BFH,0C0H,0C1H,0C2H,0C3H,0C4H,0C5H,0C6H,0C7H,0C8H,0CAH,0CBH,0CCH,0CDH,0CEH,0CFH,0D0H,0D1H,0D2H,0D3H,0D4H,0D5H,0D6H,0D7H,0D8H,0D9H,0DAH,0DBH,0DCH,0DDH,0DEH,0DFH,0E0H,0E1H,0E2H,0E3H,0E4H,0E5H,0E6H,0E7H,0E8H,0E9H,0EAH,0EBH,0ECH,0EDH,0EEH,0EFH,0F0H,0F1H,0F2H,0F3H,0F4H,0F5H,0F6H,0F7H,0F8H,0F9H,0FAH,0FBH,0FCH,0FDH: d.b := 256 * x; INC(d.st)
				ELSE d.st := -1; RETURN END
			| 1:
				CASE x + d.b OF
				| 8141H..8142H: y := x + 2AC1H
				| 8143H..8144H: y := x + 2AC2H
				| 8145H..8149H: y := x + 2AC6H
				| 814AH: y := 0AC18H
				| 814BH..814CH: y := x + 2AD3H
				| 814DH..814FH: y := x + 2AD4H
				| 8150H..8156H: y := x + 2AD5H
				| 8157H: y := 0AC2EH
				| 8158H..815AH: y := x + 2ADAH
				| 8161H..8163H: y := x + 2AD4H
				| 8164H..8165H: y := x + 2AD6H
				| 8166H..8168H: y := x + 2AD7H
				| 8169H..8172H: y := x + 2AD8H
				| 8173H: y := 0AC4CH
				| 8174H..8179H: y := x + 2ADAH
				| 817AH: y := 0AC55H
				| 8181H..8182H: y := x + 2AD5H
				| 8183H..8185H: y := x + 2AD6H
				| 8186H..8198H: y := x + 2AD7H
				| 8199H..819AH: y := x + 2AD9H
				| 819BH..819CH: y := x + 2ADAH
				| 819DH: y := 0AC79H
				| 819EH..81A2H: y := x + 2ADDH
				| 81A3H: y := 0AC82H
				| 81A4H..81A5H: y := x + 2AE3H
				| 81A6H..81A8H: y := x + 2AE7H
				| 81A9H..81ABH: y := x + 2AE8H

				| 81C5H..81C7H: y := x + 2AF9H
				| 81C8H..81C9H: y := x + 2AFAH
				| 81CAH..81CCH: y := x + 2AFBH
				| 81CDH..81CFH: y := x + 2AFCH

				ELSE d.st := -1; RETURN END;
				t[tW] := CHR(y); INC(tW);
				DEC(d.st)
			END;
			INC(fR); DEC(fLen)
		END;
		IF d.st = 0 THEN state := FALSE
		ELSIF d.st > 0 THEN state := TRUE
		ELSE HALT(100)
		END
	END Decode;

	PROCEDURE (d: Decoder) Reset;
	BEGIN d.st := 0
	END Reset;

	PROCEDURE NewDecoder* (): Codecs.Decoder;
		VAR d: Decoder;
	BEGIN
		NEW(d); d.Reset; RETURN d
	END NewDecoder;
